# GTA San Andreas — Sanny Builder Library v1.52
> Referencia compacta de opcodes/comandos para scripting CLEO en GTA SA.
> Fuente: https://library.sannybuilder.com/#/sa
> Fuente: sa.json

## Convenciones
- **VAR** = variable global | **LVAR** = variable local
- **int** = entero | **float** = decimal | **bool** = booleano | **label** = etiqueta de código
- `[in]` = parámetro de entrada | `[out]` = parámetro de salida
- **is_condition** = opcode usado como condición (IF) | **is_branch** = cambia flujo de ejecución
- **is_constructor** = crea un objeto | **is_destructor** = destruye un objeto
- **is_static** = método estático (no requiere instancia)

## Extensión: `default` (2637 comandos)

### Attractor
- `061D` **ADD_ATTRACTOR** (.Add) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float, angle:float, _p5:float, sequence:Sequence] [out: handle:Attractor] _constructor_ — Adds a ped attractor
- `061E` **CLEAR_ATTRACTOR** (.Clear) [in: self:Attractor] _destructor_
- `0680` **ADD_PEDTYPE_AS_ATTRACTOR_USER** (.AddPedTypeAsUser) [in: self:Attractor, pedType:PedType]

### Audio
- `0394` **PLAY_MISSION_PASSED_TUNE** (.PlayMissionPassedTune) [in: soundId:int] _static_ — Plays an audio file with the specified ID from the Audio directory
- `03CF` **LOAD_MISSION_AUDIO** (.LoadMissionAudio) [in: slotId:MissionAudioSlot, audioId:int] _static_ — Loads the file from the audio directory
- `03D0` **HAS_MISSION_AUDIO_LOADED** (.HasMissionAudioLoaded) [in: slotId:MissionAudioSlot] _condition, static_ — Returns true if the mission audio requested with LOAD_MISSION_AUDIO has loaded
- `03D1` **PLAY_MISSION_AUDIO** (.PlayMissionAudio) [in: slotId:MissionAudioSlot] _static_ — Plays the loaded sound (03CF)
- `03D2` **HAS_MISSION_AUDIO_FINISHED** (.HasMissionAudioFinished) [in: slotId:MissionAudioSlot] _condition, static_ — Returns true if the audio (03CF) is no longer playing
- `03D7` **SET_MISSION_AUDIO_POSITION** (.SetMissionAudioPosition) [in: slotId:MissionAudioSlot, x:float, y:float, z:float] _static_ — Sets the location of the mission audio (03CF) where it can be heard
- `040D` **CLEAR_MISSION_AUDIO** (.ClearMissionAudio) [in: slotId:MissionAudioSlot] _static_ — Unloads the mission audio (03CF), freeing game memory
- `041E` **SET_RADIO_CHANNEL** (.SetRadioChannel) [in: channel:RadioChannel] _static_ — Sets the current radio station that is playing, if the player is in a vehicle
- `043C` **SET_MUSIC_DOES_FADE** (.SetMusicDoesFade) [in: state:bool] _static_ — Sets whether sounds should fade along with the screen
- `051E` **GET_RADIO_CHANNEL** (.GetRadioChannel) [out: channel:RadioChannel] _static_ — Returns the current radio station that is being played
- `07B1` **GET_BEAT_PROXIMITY** (.GetBeatProximity) [in: offset:int] [out: beatTime:int, beatType:int, beatIndex:int] _static_ — Returns information about a beat offset from the current playback position of the active beat track (0954)
- `0949` **ATTACH_MISSION_AUDIO_TO_CHAR** (.AttachMissionAudioToChar) [in: slotId:MissionAudioSlot, handle:Char] _static_ — Sets the loaded audio to play at the char's location
- `0952` **PRELOAD_BEAT_TRACK** (.PreloadBeatTrack) [in: trackId:int] _static_ — Loads the soundtrack audio that is stored in the audio\streams\BEATS file
- `0953` **GET_BEAT_TRACK_STATUS** (.GetBeatTrackStatus) [out: status:CutsceneTrackStatus] _static_ — Returns the status of the currenly active beat track (0954)
- `0954` **PLAY_BEAT_TRACK** (.PlayBeatTrack) _static_ — Plays the last soundtrack loaded by PRELOAD_BEAT_TRACK
- `0955` **STOP_BEAT_TRACK** (.StopBeatTrack) _static_ — Stops any currently active beat track
- `097A` **REPORT_MISSION_AUDIO_EVENT_AT_POSITION** (.ReportMissionAudioEventAtPosition) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float, soundId:ScriptSound] _static_
- `097B` **REPORT_MISSION_AUDIO_EVENT_AT_OBJECT** (.ReportMissionAudioEventAtObject) [in: handle:Object, soundId:ScriptSound] _static_
- `097C` **ATTACH_MISSION_AUDIO_TO_OBJECT** (.AttachMissionAudioToObject) [in: slotId:MissionAudioSlot, handle:Object] _static_ — Sets the loaded audio to play at the object's location
- `0991` **PAUSE_CURRENT_BEAT_TRACK** (.PauseCurrentBeatTrack) [in: state:bool] _static_ — Sets whether the loaded soundtrack is paused
- `09F1` **REPORT_MISSION_AUDIO_EVENT_AT_CHAR** (.ReportMissionAudioEventAtChar) [in: handle:Char, soundId:ScriptSound] _static_
- `09F7` **REPORT_MISSION_AUDIO_EVENT_AT_CAR** (.ReportMissionAudioEventAtCar) [in: handle:Car, soundId:ScriptSound] _static_ — Plays the audio event at the car's position
- `0A16` **ATTACH_MISSION_AUDIO_TO_CAR** (.AttachMissionAudioToCar) [in: slotId:MissionAudioSlot, handle:Car] _static_ — Sets the loaded audio to play at the vehicle's location
- `0A26` **SET_RADIO_TO_PLAYERS_FAVOURITE_STATION** (.SetRadioToPlayersFavouriteStation) _static_ — Sets the radio station of the vehicle the player is currently in to the favourite station, retrieved from the stats (ID 326)

### Blip

- `0165` **CHANGE_BLIP_COLOUR** (.ChangeColor) [in: self:Blip, color:BlipColor] — Sets the blip's color

- `0168` **CHANGE_BLIP_SCALE** (.ChangeScale) [in: self:Blip, size:int] — Sets the blip's size
- `0186` **ADD_BLIP_FOR_CAR** (.AddForCar) [in: vehicle:Car] [out: handle:Blip] _constructor_ — Adds a blip and a marker to the vehicle
- `0187` **ADD_BLIP_FOR_CHAR** (.AddForChar) [in: char:Char] [out: handle:Blip] _constructor_ — Adds a blip and a marker to the character
- `0188` **ADD_BLIP_FOR_OBJECT** (.AddForObject) [in: object:Object] [out: handle:Blip] _constructor_ — Adds a blip and a marker to the object
- `018A` **ADD_BLIP_FOR_COORD** (.AddForCoord) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float] [out: handle:Blip] _constructor_ — Adds a blip to the location
- `018B` **CHANGE_BLIP_DISPLAY** (.ChangeDisplay) [in: self:Blip, display:BlipDisplay] — Changes the display of the specified blip
- `02A7` **ADD_SPRITE_BLIP_FOR_CONTACT_POINT** (.AddSpriteForContactPoint) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float, sprite:RadarSprite] [out: handle:Blip] _constructor_ — Adds a long range sprite blip and sphere to the contact point that is not displayed while on mission
- `02A8` **ADD_SPRITE_BLIP_FOR_COORD** (.AddSpriteForCoord) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float, sprite:RadarSprite] [out: handle:Blip] _constructor_ — Adds a sprite blip to the location
- `03DC` **ADD_BLIP_FOR_PICKUP** (.AddForPickup) [in: pickup:Pickup] [out: handle:Blip] _constructor_ — Adds a blip and a marker to the pickup
- `04CE` **ADD_SHORT_RANGE_SPRITE_BLIP_FOR_COORD** (.AddShortRangeSpriteForCoord) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float, sprite:RadarSprite] [out: handle:Blip] _constructor_ — Adds a sprite blip for the specified coordinates
- `0570` **ADD_SHORT_RANGE_SPRITE_BLIP_FOR_CONTACT_POINT** (.AddShortRangeSpriteForContactPoint) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float, sprite:RadarSprite] [out: handle:Blip] _constructor_ — Adds a short range sprite blip and sphere to the contact point that is not displayed while on mission
- `06C4` **ADD_BLIP_FOR_SEARCHLIGHT** (.AddForSearchlight) [in: searchlight:Searchlight] [out: handle:Blip] _constructor_ — Creates a blip indicating the searchlights position on the radar
- `075C` **DOES_BLIP_EXIST** (.DoesExist) [in: handle:any] _condition, static_ — Returns true if the handle is a valid blip handle
- `07BF` **SET_BLIP_ALWAYS_DISPLAY_ON_ZOOMED_RADAR** (.SetAlwaysDisplayOnZoomedRadar) [in: self:Blip, state:bool] — Sets whether the tracking blip will remain regardless of the entities existance
- `07E0` **SET_BLIP_AS_FRIENDLY** (.SetAsFriendly) [in: self:Blip, state:bool]
- `0888` **ADD_BLIP_FOR_DEAD_CHAR** (.AddForDeadChar) [in: char:Char] [out: handle:Blip] _constructor_ — Adds a blip and a marker to the character (identical to 0187)
- `08DC` **SET_BLIP_ENTRY_EXIT** (.SetEntryExit) [in: self:Blip, x:float, y:float, radius:float] — Assigns the blip to the specified entrance/exit marker
- `08FB` **SET_COORD_BLIP_APPEARANCE** (.SetCoordAppearance) [in: self:Blip, color:CoordAppearance] — Works similar to 0165, except this command does not work on tracking blips, has different colors and does not support direct RGBA setting

### Boat
- `02D3` **BOAT_GOTO_COORDS** (.Goto) [in: self:Boat, x:float, y:float, z:float] — Makes the boat sail to the location
- `02D4` **BOAT_STOP** (.Stop) [in: self:Boat] — Turns off the car's engine
- `02DB` **SET_BOAT_CRUISE_SPEED** (.SetCruiseSpeed) [in: self:Boat, maxSpeed:float] — Sets the boat's max speed
- `0323` **ANCHOR_BOAT** (.Anchor) [in: self:Boat, state:bool] — Makes the boat stay motionless in the water

### Camera
- `0003` **SHAKE_CAM** (.Shake) [in: intensity:int] _static_ — Shakes the camera with the given intensity
- `00C2` **IS_POINT_ON_SCREEN** (.IsPointOnScreen) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float, radius:float] _condition, static_ — Returns true if any part of the radius of the specified point is visible on screen
- `0158` **POINT_CAMERA_AT_CAR** (.PointAtCar) [in: vehicle:Car, mode:CameraMode, switchStyle:SwitchType] _static_ — Attaches the camera to the specified vehicle
- `0159` **POINT_CAMERA_AT_CHAR** (.PointAtChar) [in: char:Char, mode:CameraMode, switchStyle:SwitchType] _static_ — Attaches the camera to the specified character
- `015A` **RESTORE_CAMERA** (.Restore) _static_ — Restores the camera to its usual position
- `015F` **SET_FIXED_CAMERA_POSITION** (.SetFixedPosition) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float, upVecOffsetX:float, upVecOffsetY:float, upVecOffsetZ:float] _static_ — Sets the fixed camera's position and up vector offset
- `0160` **POINT_CAMERA_AT_POINT** (.PointAtPoint) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float, switchStyle:SwitchType] _static_ — Points the camera at the specified location and applies the position set by 0159
- `0169` **SET_FADING_COLOUR** (.SetFadingColor) [in: r:int, g:int, b:int] _static_ — Sets the RGB color of the fade command (016A)
- `016A` **DO_FADE** (.DoFade) [in: time:int, direction:Fade] _static_ — Fades the screen for the specified time
- `016B` **GET_FADING_STATUS** (.GetFadingStatus) _condition, static_ — Returns true if the screen is fading (016A)
- `02EB` **RESTORE_CAMERA_JUMPCUT** (.RestoreJumpcut) _static_ — Restores the camera, putting it back behind the player
- `032A` **SET_CAMERA_ZOOM** (.SetZoom) [in: zoom:int] _static_ — Sets how far behind the camera is from the player
- `0373` **SET_CAMERA_BEHIND_PLAYER** (.SetBehindPlayer) _static_ — Puts the camera behind the player
- `03C8` **SET_CAMERA_IN_FRONT_OF_PLAYER** (.SetInFrontOfPlayer) _static_ — Puts the camera in front of the player, pointing towards the player
- `041D` **SET_NEAR_CLIP** (.SetNearClip) [in: distance:float] _static_ — Sets camera minimum drawing distance
- `0454` **GET_DEBUG_CAMERA_COORDINATES** (.GetDebugCoordinates) [out: x:float, y:float, z:float] _static_ — Returns the debug camera position
- `0460` **SET_INTERPOLATION_PARAMETERS** (.SetInterpolationParameters) [in: interpolationToStopMoving:float, time:int] _static_ — Sets how long the camera transition will last
- `0463` **GET_DEBUG_CAMERA_POINT_AT** (.GetDebugPointAt) [out: x:float, y:float, z:float] _static_ — Stores the location the debug camera is pointing to
- `0679` **ATTACH_CAMERA_TO_VEHICLE** (.AttachToVehicle) [in: handle:Car, xOffset:float, yOffset:float, zOffset:float, xRotation:float, yRotation:float, zRotation:float, tilt:float, switchStyle:SwitchType] _static_ — Keeps the camera relative to the car with the specified offset
- `067A` **ATTACH_CAMERA_TO_VEHICLE_LOOK_AT_VEHICLE** (.AttachToVehicleLookAtVehicle) [in: handle:Car, xOffset:float, yOffset:float, zOffset:float, vehicle:Car, tilt:float, switchStyle:SwitchType] _static_ — Puts the camera on the vehicle like in 0679
- `067B` **ATTACH_CAMERA_TO_VEHICLE_LOOK_AT_CHAR** (.AttachToVehicleLookAtChar) [in: car:Car, xOffset:float, yOffset:float, zOffset:float, char:Char, tilt:float, switchStyle:SwitchType] _static_ — Attaches the camera to the vehicle and points it at the specified character
- `067C` **ATTACH_CAMERA_TO_CHAR** (.AttachToChar) [in: handle:Char, xOffset:float, yOffset:float, zOffset:float, xRotation:float, yRotation:float, zRotation:float, tilt:float, switchStyle:SwitchType] _static_ — Keeps the camera relative to the char with the specified offset
- `067D` **ATTACH_CAMERA_TO_CHAR_LOOK_AT_VEHICLE** (.AttachToCharLookAtVehicle) [in: char:Char, xOffset:float, yOffset:float, zOffset:float, vehicle:Car, tilt:float, switchStyle:SwitchType] _static_
- `067E` **ATTACH_CAMERA_TO_CHAR_LOOK_AT_CHAR** (.AttachToCharLookAtChar) [in: handle:Char, xOffset:float, yOffset:float, zOffset:float, char:Char, tilt:float, switchStyle:SwitchType] _static_ — Puts the camera on the character like with 067C
- `068D` **GET_ACTIVE_CAMERA_COORDINATES** (.GetActiveCoordinates) [out: x:float, y:float, z:float] _static_ — Stores the cameras coordinates
- `068E` **GET_ACTIVE_CAMERA_POINT_AT** (.GetActivePointAt) [out: x:float, y:float, z:float] _static_ — Gets the coordinates the camera is pointing to
- `06E0` **SET_TWO_PLAYER_CAMERA_MODE** (.SetTwoPlayerMode) [in: state:bool] _static_ — Enables the cooperative camera mode
- `0801` **GET_CAMERA_FOV** (.GetFov) [out: fov:float] _static_ — Returns the cameras field of view
- `0822` **SET_FIRST_PERSON_IN_CAR_CAMERA_MODE** (.SetFirstPersonInCarMode) [in: state:bool] _static_ — Enables vehicle bumper view for the camera
- `0834` **DO_CAMERA_BUMP** (.DoBump) [in: xOffset:float, yOffset:float] _static_ — Bumps the camera in the specified direction as if it had collided
- `0920` **CAMERA_SET_VECTOR_TRACK** (.SetVectorTrack) [in: fromX:float, fromY:float, fromZ:float, toX:float, toY:float, toZ:float, time:int, ease:bool] _static_ — Makes the camera point at the first coordinates and then rotate to point at the second coordinates
- `0922` **CAMERA_SET_LERP_FOV** (.SetLerpFov) [in: from:float, to:float, time:int, ease:bool] _static_ — Sets the cameras zoom factors
- `0924` **SET_DARKNESS_EFFECT** (.SetDarknessEffect) [in: enable:bool, pitchBlack:int] _static_ — Darkens the game
- `0925` **CAMERA_RESET_NEW_SCRIPTABLES** (.ResetNewScriptables) _static_ — Stops the camera propagating, interpolating, shaking and zooming
- `092F` **CAMERA_PERSIST_TRACK** (.PersistTrack) [in: state:bool] _static_ — Locks the camera target point in position after propagating
- `0930` **CAMERA_PERSIST_POS** (.PersistPos) [in: state:bool] _static_ — Locks the cameras position
- `0931` **CAMERA_PERSIST_FOV** (.PersistFov) [in: state:bool] _static_ — Locks the zoom level after the camera has finished zooming
- `0933` **CAMERA_IS_VECTOR_MOVE_RUNNING** (.IsVectorMoveRunning) _condition, static_ — Returns true if the camera is moving in position
- `0934` **CAMERA_IS_VECTOR_TRACK_RUNNING** (.IsVectorTrackRunning) _condition, static_ — Returns true if the camera is moving in angle
- `0936` **CAMERA_SET_VECTOR_MOVE** (.SetVectorMove) [in: fromX:float, fromY:float, fromZ:float, toX:float, toY:float, toZ:float, time:int, ease:bool] _static_ — Puts the camera at the position of the first passed coordinates and moves it to the second passed coordinates
- `093D` **SET_CINEMA_CAMERA** (.SetCinema) [in: state:bool] _static_ — Locks the camera on cinematic vehicle mode
- `0944` **SET_CAMERA_IN_FRONT_OF_CHAR** (.SetInFrontOfChar) [in: handle:Char] _static_ — Puts the camera in front of the specified character
- `099C` **CAMERA_SET_SHAKE_SIMULATION_SIMPLE** (.SetShakeSimulationSimple) [in: type:int, timeInMs:float, intensity:float] _static_ — Jiggles the camera in a variety of different ways
- `09AD` **SET_PLAYER_IN_CAR_CAMERA_MODE** (.SetPlayerInCarMode) [in: mode:int] _static_ — Changes the camera mode on the current vehicle, just like when the user presses the 'change view' key
- `09EC` **ALLOW_FIXED_CAMERA_COLLISION** (.AllowFixedCollision) [in: state:bool] _static_ — Makes the camera remain behind the player when in any garage
- `09EF` **SET_VEHICLE_CAMERA_TWEAK** (.SetVehicleTweak) [in: modelId:model_vehicle, distance:float, altitude:float, angle:float] _static_ — Sets the position the camera automatically moves to while driving a vehicle of the specified type
- `09F0` **RESET_VEHICLE_CAMERA_TWEAK** (.ResetVehicleTweak) _static_ — Resets any changes made with 09EF
- `0A1E` **TAKE_PHOTO** (.TakePhoto) [in: _p1:bool] _static_ — Takes a screenshot of the screen without any HUD elements and stores the file in the "GTA San Andreas User FilesGallery" folder
- `0A25` **SET_CAMERA_POSITION_UNFIXED** (.SetPositionUnfixed) [in: xOffset:float, yOffset:float] _static_ — Sets the position of the camera to an offset of the targeted entity
- `0A2F` **SET_PHOTO_CAMERA_EFFECT** (.SetPhotoEffect) [in: state:bool] _static_ — Puts the camera in first-person mode if the player is holding a weapon with a first-person shooting mode (such as a sniper rifle or camera)
- `0A39` **GET_PLAYER_IN_CAR_CAMERA_MODE** (.GetPlayerInCarMode) [out: mode:int] _static_ — Gets the players chosen camera mode of the current vehicle

### Car
- `00A5` **CREATE_CAR** (.Create) [in: modelId:model_vehicle, x:float, y:float, z:float] [out: handle:Car] _constructor_ — Creates a vehicle at the specified location, with the specified model
- `00A6` **DELETE_CAR** (.Delete) [in: self:Car] _destructor_ — Removes the vehicle from the game
- `00A7` **CAR_GOTO_COORDINATES** (.GotoCoordinates) [in: self:Car, x:float, y:float, z:float] — Makes the AI drive to the specified location by any means
- `00A8` **CAR_WANDER_RANDOMLY** (.WanderRandomly) [in: self:Car] — Clears any current tasks the vehicle has and makes it drive around aimlessly
- `00A9` **CAR_SET_IDLE** (.SetIdle) [in: self:Car] — Sets the car's mission to idle (MISSION_NONE), stopping any driving activity
- `00AA` **GET_CAR_COORDINATES** (.GetCoordinates) [in: self:Car] [out: x:float, y:float, z:float] — Returns the vehicle's coordinates

- `0919` **SET_CAR_LIGHTS_ON** (.SetLightsOn) [in: self:Car, state:bool] — Sets whether the vehicle's lights are on
- `0939` **ATTACH_CAR_TO_OBJECT** (.AttachToObject) [in: self:Car, handle:Object, xOffset:float, yOffset:float, zOffset:float, xRotation:float, yRotation:float, zRotation:float] — Attaches the car to object with offset and rotation
- `0957` **VEHICLE_DOES_PROVIDE_COVER** (.DoesProvideCover) [in: self:Car, state:bool] — Sets whether characters in combat will choose to use the vehicle as cover from gunfire
- `095E` **CONTROL_CAR_DOOR** (.ControlDoor) [in: self:Car, door:CarDoor, state:CarDoorState, angle:float] — Sets the car's door angle and latch state

- `09E9` **GIVE_NON_PLAYER_CAR_NITRO** (.GiveNonPlayerNitro) [in: self:Car] — Makes the car have one nitro

### CarGenerator
- `014B` **CREATE_CAR_GENERATOR** (.Create) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float, heading:float, modelId:model_vehicle, primaryColor:int, secondaryColor:int, forceSpawn:bool, alarmChance:int, doorLockChance:int, minDelay:int, maxDelay:int] [out: handle:CarGenerator] _constructor_ — Initializes a parked car generator (modelId -1 selects a random vehicle from the local popcycle)
- `014C` **SWITCH_CAR_GENERATOR** (.Switch) [in: self:CarGenerator, amount:int] — Specifies the number of times the car generator spawns a car (101 - infinite)
- `0732` **SUPPRESS_CAR_MODEL** (.SuppressCarModel) [in: model:model_vehicle] _static_ — Prevents the specified car model from spawning for car generators

- `09E2` **CREATE_CAR_GENERATOR_WITH_PLATE** (.CreateWithPlate) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float, heading:float, modelId:model_vehicle, primaryColor:int, secondaryColor:int, forceSpawn:bool, alarmChance:int, doorLockChance:int, minDelay:int, maxDelay:int, plateName:string] [out: handle:CarGenerator] _constructor_ — Creates a parked car generator with a number plate (modelId -1 selects a random vehicle from the local popcycle)
- `0A17` **SET_HAS_BEEN_OWNED_FOR_CAR_GENERATOR** (.SetHasBeenOwned) [in: self:CarGenerator, state:bool] — Sets whether the player will not receive a wanted level when entering a vehicle from this generator when the police is around

### Mission
- `00D8` **MISSION_HAS_FINISHED** (.Finish) _static_ — Resets multiple settings that are usually set during missions and in some scripts
- `0417` **LOAD_AND_LAUNCH_MISSION_INTERNAL** (.LoadAndLaunchInternal) [in: index:int] _static_ — Loads a mission from the list defined in the main.scm header
- `045C` **FAIL_CURRENT_MISSION** (.Fail) _static_ — Terminates the active mission by executing its mission cleanup routine

### Mouse
- `0A4A` **GET_PC_MOUSE_MOVEMENT** (.GetMovement) [out: deltaX:float, deltaY:float] _static_ — Gives the offset of the mouse or right thumbstick movement
- `0A4C` **IS_MOUSE_USING_VERTICAL_INVERSION** (.IsUsingVerticalInversion) _condition, static_ — Returns true if the players settings are set to invert the mouse

### Object
- `0107` **CREATE_OBJECT** (.Create) [in: modelId:model_object, x:float, y:float, z:float] [out: handle:Object] _constructor_ — Creates an object at the specified location, with the specified model
- `0108` **DELETE_OBJECT** (.Delete) [in: self:Object] _destructor_ — Destroys the object, freeing game memory
- `0176` **GET_OBJECT_HEADING** (.GetHeading) [in: self:Object] [out: heading:float] — Returns the object's heading (z-angle)
- `0177` **SET_OBJECT_HEADING** (.SetHeading) [in: self:Object, heading:float] — Sets the object's heading (z-angle)
- `01BB` **GET_OBJECT_COORDINATES** (.GetCoordinates) [in: self:Object] [out: x:float, y:float, z:float] — Returns the object's coordinates
- `01BC` **SET_OBJECT_COORDINATES** (.SetCoordinates) [in: self:Object, x:float, y:float, z:float] — Puts the object at the specified location
- `01C4` **MARK_OBJECT_AS_NO_LONGER_NEEDED** (.MarkAsNoLongerNeeded) [in: self:Object] — Allows the object to be deleted by the game if necessary, and also removes it from the mission cleanup list, if applicable
- `01C7` **DONT_REMOVE_OBJECT** (.DontRemove) [in: self:Object] — Removes the object from the mission cleanup list, preventing it from being deleted when the mission ends
- `029B` **CREATE_OBJECT_NO_OFFSET** (.CreateNoOffset) [in: modelId:model_object, x:float, y:float, z:float] [out: handle:Object] _constructor_ — Creates an object without offset at the location
- `02CC` **IS_OBJECT_ON_SCREEN** (.IsOnScreen) [in: self:Object] _condition_ — Returns true if the object is visible
- `034D` **ROTATE_OBJECT** (.Rotate) [in: self:Object, fromAngle:float, toAngle:float, collisionCheck:bool] _condition_ — Rotates the object from one angle to another, optionally accounting for a collision during the rotation
- `034E` **SLIDE_OBJECT** (.Slide) [in: self:Object, posX:float, posY:float, posZ:float, speedX:float, speedY:float, speedZ:float, collisionCheck:bool] _condition_ — Animates object movement toward specified coordinates. Returns true if the object has finished moving
- `035C` **PLACE_OBJECT_RELATIVE_TO_CAR** (.PlaceRelativeToCar) [in: self:Object, vehicle:Car, xOffset:float, yOffset:float, zOffset:float] — Places the object at an offset from the car
- `035D` **MAKE_OBJECT_TARGETTABLE** (.MakeTargetable) [in: self:Object, state:bool] — Sets whether the object can be targeted (auto-aimed) or not
- `0366` **HAS_OBJECT_BEEN_DAMAGED** (.HasBeenDamaged) [in: self:Object] _condition_ — Returns true if the object is damaged
- `0381` **SET_OBJECT_VELOCITY** (.SetVelocity) [in: self:Object, xSpeed:float, ySpeed:float, zSpeed:float] — Sets the object's velocity
- `0382` **SET_OBJECT_COLLISION** (.SetCollision) [in: self:Object, state:bool] — Sets the object's collision detection
- `038C` **ADD_TO_OBJECT_VELOCITY** (.AddToVelocity) [in: self:Object, x:float, y:float, z:float] — Adds the given vector to the object's velocity (0381)
- `0392` **SET_OBJECT_DYNAMIC** (.SetDynamic) [in: self:Object, state:bool] — Defines whether or not the object is moveable
- `03CA` **DOES_OBJECT_EXIST** (.DoesExist) [in: handle:any] _condition, static_ — Returns true if the handle is a valid object handle
- `0400` **GET_OFFSET_FROM_OBJECT_IN_WORLD_COORDS** (.GetOffsetInWorldCoords) [in: self:Object, xOffset:float, yOffset:float, zOffset:float] [out: x:float, y:float, z:float] — Returns the object's coordinates with an offset
- `0418` **SET_OBJECT_DRAW_LAST** (.SetDrawLast) [in: self:Object, state:bool] — Sets the specified object to always draw on top of other objects
- `0453` **SET_OBJECT_ROTATION** (.SetRotation) [in: self:Object, x:float, y:float, z:float] — Sets the object rotation along X, Y and Z axis
- `04D9` **SET_OBJECT_RECORDS_COLLISIONS** (.SetRecordsCollisions) [in: self:Object, state:bool] — Enables the use of collision checking for the object
- `04DA` **HAS_OBJECT_COLLIDED_WITH_ANYTHING** (.HasCollidedWithAnything) [in: self:Object] _condition_ — Returns true if the object has collided
- `04E5` **LOCATE_OBJECT_2D** (.Locate2D) [in: self:Object, x:float, y:float, xRadius:float, yRadius:float, drawSphere:bool] _condition_ — Returns true if the object is near the specified coordinates
- `04E6` **LOCATE_OBJECT_3D** (.Locate3D) [in: self:Object, x:float, y:float, z:float, xRadius:float, yRadius:float, zRadius:float, drawSphere:bool] _condition_ — Returns true if the object is near the specified point
- `04E7` **IS_OBJECT_IN_WATER** (.IsInWater) [in: self:Object] _condition_ — Returns true if the object is in water

- `04EA` **IS_OBJECT_IN_AREA_3D** (.IsInArea3D) [in: self:Object, leftBottomX:float, leftBottomY:float, leftBottomZ:float, rightTopX:float, rightTopY:float, rightTopZ:float, drawSphere:bool] _condition_ — Returns true if the object is in the specified area
- `050E` **SORT_OUT_OBJECT_COLLISION_WITH_CAR** (.SortOutCollisionWithCar) [in: self:Object, handle:Car] — Makes the specified car have no collision with the specified object
- `0550` **FREEZE_OBJECT_POSITION** (.FreezePosition) [in: self:Object, state:bool] — Sets whether the object's position remains unchanged
- `0566` **SET_OBJECT_AREA_VISIBLE** (.SetAreaVisible) [in: self:Object, areaId:int] — Sets the visibility of the object to the specified interior
- `059F` **GET_OBJECT_VELOCITY** (.GetVelocity) [in: self:Object] [out: x:float, y:float, z:float] — Returns the object's X, Y, and Z velocity
- `05A1` **ADD_TO_OBJECT_ROTATION_VELOCITY** (.AddToRotationVelocity) [in: self:Object, x:float, y:float, z:float] — Sets the object's rotation velocity from the center of its body
- `05A2` **SET_OBJECT_ROTATION_VELOCITY** (.SetRotationVelocity) [in: self:Object, x:float, y:float, z:float] — Sets the object's rotation velocity with frame sync applied?

### Pickup
- `0213` **CREATE_PICKUP** (.Create) [in: modelId:model_object, pickupType:PickupType, x:float, y:float, z:float] [out: handle:Pickup] _constructor_ — Creates a pickup with the given model and type

### Text

- `0341` **SET_TEXT_JUSTIFY** (.SetJustify) [in: state:bool] _static_ — Sets the text to be drawn justified, which means the text will wrap in order to fill an even rectangle of space

### Train
- `06D8` **CREATE_MISSION_TRAIN** (.Create) [in: type:int, x:float, y:float, z:float, direction:bool] [out: handle:Train] _constructor_ — Creates a script handled train from a predefined type (the type dictates how long the train is and the varieties of carriages) and sets the direction for the train to head in
- `06DC` **SET_TRAIN_SPEED** (.SetSpeed) [in: self:Train, speed:float] — Sets the trains acceleration
- `06DD` **SET_TRAIN_CRUISE_SPEED** (.SetCruiseSpeed) [in: self:Train, speed:float] — Sets the trains speed
- `06DE` **GET_TRAIN_CABOOSE** (.GetCaboose) [in: self:Train] [out: caboose:Car] — Gets the handle of the last carriage (known as the "caboose")
- `078A` **GET_TRAIN_CARRIAGE** (.GetCarriage) [in: self:Train, number:int] [out: carriage:Car] — Gets the nth train carriage
- `07BD` **DELETE_MISSION_TRAIN** (.Delete) [in: self:Train] _destructor_ — Removes the specified script created train
- `07BE` **MARK_MISSION_TRAIN_AS_NO_LONGER_NEEDED** (.MarkAsNoLongerNeeded) [in: self:Train] — Removes the specified script created train from the list of trains that the game shouldn't delete
- `07C7` **SET_MISSION_TRAIN_COORDINATES** (.SetCoordinates) [in: self:Train, x:float, y:float, z:float] — Puts the train on the rails nearest to the specified coordinates
- `0981` **HAS_TRAIN_DERAILED** (.HasDerailed) [in: self:Train] _condition_ — Returns true if the train has derailed (usually from going too fast)
- `09CF` **SET_TRAIN_FORCED_TO_SLOW_DOWN** (.SetForcedToSlowDown) [in: self:Train, state:bool] — Sets whether the train should stop at each station it encounters
- `09E3` **FIND_TRAIN_DIRECTION** (.FindDirection) [in: self:Train] _condition_ — Returns true if the train is travelling clockwise, around San Andreas
- `0A06` **IS_NEXT_STATION_ALLOWED** (.IsNextStationAllowed) [in: self:Train] _condition_ — Returns true if the next station is accessible (at the start of the game, railroad blocks prevent the player from travelling to stations whose area is not unlocked)
- `0A07` **SKIP_TO_NEXT_ALLOWED_STATION** (.SkipToNextAllowedStation) [in: self:Train] — Puts the script created train at the next allowed station

### Zone
- `02DD` **GET_RANDOM_CHAR_IN_ZONE** (.GetRandomChar) [in: zone:zone_key, civilian:bool, gang:bool, criminalOrProstitute:bool] [out: handle:Char] _constructor_ — Gets a random character in the specified zone whose pedtype matches the specified values

- `076B` **GET_ZONE_DEALER_STRENGTH** (.GetDealerStrength) [in: zone:zone_key] [out: density:int] _static_ — Returns the drug dealer density of the specified zone
- `076C` **SET_ZONE_GANG_STRENGTH** (.SetGangStrength) [in: zoneId:zone_key, gangId:GangType, density:int] _static_ — Sets the density of the gang members in the specified zone
- `076D` **GET_ZONE_GANG_STRENGTH** (.GetGangStrength) [in: zone:zone_key, gangId:GangType] [out: density:int] _static_ — Returns the density of the gang members in the specified zone
- `0843` **GET_NAME_OF_ZONE** (.GetTextKey) [in: x:float, y:float, z:float] [out: key:gxt_key] _static_ — Returns the GXT key associated with the zone at the specified coordinates
- `0874` **SET_ZONE_POPULATION_RACE** (.SetPopulationRace) [in: zone:zone_key, races:RaceSet] _static_ — Sets which races will inhabit this zone

- `08D3` **GET_CURRENT_POPULATION_ZONE_TYPE** (.GetCurrentPopulationZoneType) [out: type:ZoneType] _static_ — Returns the population type in the zone the player is currently in

- `09B7` **SET_ZONE_NO_COPS** (.SetNoCops) [in: zone:zone_key, state:bool] _static_ — Sets whether cops should be prevented from spawning in the specified area
- `0A24` **SET_DISABLE_MILITARY_ZONES** (.SetDisableMilitaryZones) [in: state:bool] _static_ — Causes the players wanted level to be set at 4 when in restricted areas

### (sin clase)
- `0000` **NOP** — Has no effect and is commonly used to pad CLEO scripts with extra space to avoid the jump-at-zero-offset bug
- `0001` **WAIT** [in: time:int] — Pauses the script execution for specified amount of time in milliseconds
- `0002` **GOTO** [in: _:label] _branch, segment_ — Transfers the script execution to the label unconditionally
- `0004` **SET_VAR_INT** `=` [in: _:int, _:int] — Sets the integer value of the VAR
- `0005` **SET_VAR_FLOAT** `=` [in: _:float, _:float] — Sets the float value of the VAR
- `0006` **SET_LVAR_INT** `=` [in: _:int, _:int] — Sets the integer value of the LVAR
- `0007` **SET_LVAR_FLOAT** `=` [in: _:float, _:float] — Sets the float value of the LVAR
- `0008` **ADD_VAL_TO_INT_VAR** `+` [in: _:int, _:int] — Adds the value to the value of the int VAR
- `0009` **ADD_VAL_TO_FLOAT_VAR** `+` [in: _:float, _:float] — Adds the value to the value of the float VAR
- `000A` **ADD_VAL_TO_INT_LVAR** `+` [in: _:int, _:int] — Adds the value to the value of the integer LVAR
- `000B` **ADD_VAL_TO_FLOAT_LVAR** `+` [in: _:float, _:float] — Adds the value to the value of the float LVAR
- `000C` **SUB_VAL_FROM_INT_VAR** `-` [in: _:int, _:int] — Subtracts the value from the value of the integer VAR
- `000D` **SUB_VAL_FROM_FLOAT_VAR** `-` [in: _:float, _:float] — Subtracts the value from the value of the float VAR
- `000E` **SUB_VAL_FROM_INT_LVAR** `-` [in: _:int, _:int] — Subtracts the value from the value of the int LVAR
- `000F` **SUB_VAL_FROM_FLOAT_LVAR** `-` [in: _:float, _:float] — Subtracts the value from the value of the float LVAR
- `0010` **MULT_INT_VAR_BY_VAL** `*` [in: _:int, _:int] — Multiplies the int VAR by the value
- `0011` **MULT_FLOAT_VAR_BY_VAL** `*` [in: _:float, _:float] — Multiplies the float VAR by the value
- `0012` **MULT_INT_LVAR_BY_VAL** `*` [in: _:int, _:int] — Multiplies the int LVAR by the value
- `0013` **MULT_FLOAT_LVAR_BY_VAL** `*` [in: _:float, _:float] — Multiplies the float LVAR by the value
- `0014` **DIV_INT_VAR_BY_VAL** `/` [in: _:int, _:int] — Divides the int VAR by the value
- `0015` **DIV_FLOAT_VAR_BY_VAL** `/` [in: _:float, _:float] — Divides the float VAR by the value
- `0016` **DIV_INT_LVAR_BY_VAL** `/` [in: _:int, _:int] — Divides the int LVAR by the value
- `0017` **DIV_FLOAT_LVAR_BY_VAL** `/` [in: _:float, _:float] — Divides the float LVAR by the value

### Memory

- `0EE3` **WRITE_STRUCT_OFFSET_MULTI** (.WriteStructOffsetMulti) [in: address:int, offset:int, count:int, size:int, params:arguments] _static_ — Writes the value at the given offset from the memory address multiple times as array/vector

- `0BE7` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_READ** (.Read) [in: self:SampBitstream, dataType:SampBitStreamDataType] [out: value:any] _condition_ — Reads a value with datatype and datasize at the "read pointer" of the specified bitstream , then advances its "read pointer" by the same size
- `0BE8` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_READ_ARRAY** (.ReadArray) [in: self:SampBitstream, buffer:int, size:int] _condition_ — Stores an array of bytes from the Bitstream to buffer
- `0BE9` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_RESET_READ_POINTER** (.ResetReadPtr) [in: self:SampBitstream] _condition_ — Resets the read pointer of the BitStream. Setting "write offset = 0"
- `0BEA` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_RESET_WRITE_POINTER** (.ResetWritePtr) [in: self:SampBitstream] _condition_ — Resets (THIS COMMAND IS BUGGED, SETS THE WRITE POINTER AT THE BEGINNING OF THE DATA ( WRITE OFFSET = 0) WHICH IS WRONG. DO NOT USE) the value write pointer in the BitStream
- `0BEB` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_SKIP_BITS** (.SkipBits) [in: self:SampBitstream, bitCount:int] _condition_ — Increases both its "read pointer" and "write pointer" of the Bitstream by the specified bit count
- `0BEC` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_SET_WRITE_OFFSET** (.SetWriteOffset) [in: self:SampBitstream, offset:int] _condition_ — Sets the write offset of the BitStream
- `0BED` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_SET_READ_OFFSET** (.SetReadPtr) [in: self:SampBitstream, offset:int] _condition_ — Sets the read offset of the BitStream
- `0BEE` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_GET_NUMBER_OF_BITS_USED** (.GetBitsUsed) [in: self:SampBitstream] [out: usedBits:int] — Returns the number of used bits in the BitStream
- `0BEF` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_GET_NUMBER_OF_BYTES_USED** (.GetBytesUsed) [in: self:SampBitstream] [out: usedBytes:int] _condition_ — Returns the number of bytes used in the BitStream
- `0BF0` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_GET_NUMBER_OF_UNREAD_BITS** (.GetUnreadBits) [in: self:SampBitstream] [out: unreadBits:int] _condition_ — Returns the number of unread bits in the BitStream
- `0BF1` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_GET_WRITE_OFFSET** (.GetWriteOffset) [in: self:SampBitstream] [out: offset:int] _condition_ — Returns the current write offset of the BitStream
- `0BF2` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_GET_READ_OFFSET** (.GetReadOffset) [in: self:SampBitstream] [out: offset:int] _condition_ — Returns the current read offset of the BitStream
- `0BF3` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_GET_DATA_POINTER** (.GetDataPtr) [in: self:SampBitstream] [out: address:int] _condition_ — Returns a pointer to the BitStream's data
- `0BF4` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_DECODE_COMPRESSED_STRING** (.DecodeCString) [in: self:SampBitstream, buffer:int, buffersize:int] _condition_ — Decrypts a compressed string (CString) from the bitstream then stores this to the buffer
- `0BF5` **SAMP_RAKNET_BITSTREAM_ENCODE_STRING** (.EncodeString) [in: self:SampBitstream, buffer:int, bufferSize:int] _condition_ — Encrypts a string stored in the buffer then stores this compressed string (CString) to the bitstream

- `2504` **SET_AUDIO_STREAM_VOLUME_WITH_TRANSITION** (.SetVolumeWithTransition) [in: self:AudioStream, volume:float, timeMs:int] — Changes stream volume with smooth transition
- `2505` **SET_AUDIO_STREAM_SPEED_WITH_TRANSITION** (.SetSpeedWithTransition) [in: self:AudioStream, speed:float, timeMs:int] — Changes stream speed with smooth transition. Pauses/Starts stream playback if neccesarry
- `2507` **GET_AUDIO_STREAM_PROGRESS** (.GetProgress) [in: self:AudioStream] [out: progress:float] — Gets audio stream playback progress as value from 0.0 to 1.0
- `2508` **SET_AUDIO_STREAM_PROGRESS** (.SetProgress) [in: self:AudioStream, progress:float] — Sets audio stream playback position. Progress range is from 0.0 to 1.0
- `2509` **GET_AUDIO_STREAM_TYPE** (.GetType) [in: self:AudioStream] [out: type:AudioStreamType] — Returns current volume settings type group of the stream
- `250A` **SET_AUDIO_STREAM_TYPE** (.SetType) [in: self:AudioStream, type:AudioStreamType] — Sets which game's master volume settings the stream should follow
- `250B` **GET_AUDIO_STREAM_PROGRESS_SECONDS** (.GetProgressSeconds) [in: self:AudioStream] [out: progress:float] — Returns current playback progress in seconds. Does not take in consideration current stream's playback speed
- `250C` **SET_AUDIO_STREAM_PROGRESS_SECONDS** (.SetProgressSeconds) [in: self:AudioStream, progress:float] — Sets current playback progress in seconds. Does not take in consideration current stream's playback speed

### AudioStream3D
- `0AC1` **LOAD_3D_AUDIO_STREAM** (.Load) [in: audioFileName:string] [out: handle:AudioStream3D] _condition, constructor_ — Loads an audio file and creates a new 3d audio stream (see 0AAC)
- `0AC2` **SET_PLAY_3D_AUDIO_STREAM_AT_COORDS** (.SetPlayAtCoords) [in: self:AudioStream3D, x:float, y:float, z:float] — Sets sound source position to specific world location
- `0AC3` **SET_PLAY_3D_AUDIO_STREAM_AT_OBJECT** (.SetPlayAtObject) [in: self:AudioStream3D, object:Object] — Attaches sound source to the object
- `0AC4` **SET_PLAY_3D_AUDIO_STREAM_AT_CHAR** (.SetPlayAtChar) [in: self:AudioStream3D, char:Char] — Attaches sound source to the character
- `0AC5` **SET_PLAY_3D_AUDIO_STREAM_AT_CAR** (.SetPlayAtCar) [in: self:AudioStream3D, car:Car] — Attaches sound source to the vehicle
- `2506` **SET_AUDIO_STREAM_SOURCE_SIZE** (.SetSourceSize) [in: self:AudioStream3D, radius:float] — Sets size of 3d audio stream sound source in the world. Volume will not decay within the specified distance

## Extensión: `bitwise` (15 comandos)

### Math
- `0B1E` **SIGN_EXTEND** (.SignExtend) [in: value:int, fromSize:int] _static_ — Extends a 1-, 2- or 3-byte long integer value to a 4-byte (32-bit), while preserving the sign (+/-)

### (sin clase)
- `0B10` **BIT_AND** `&` [in: _:int, _:int] [out: _:int] — Returns a result of the bitwise AND operation on the corresponding bits of the first and second operands
- `0B11` **BIT_OR** `|` [in: _:int, _:int] [out: _:int] — Returns a result of the bitwise OR operation on the corresponding bits of the first and second operands
- `0B12` **BIT_XOR** `^` [in: _:int, _:int] [out: _:int] — Returns a result of the bitwise XOR operation on the corresponding bits of the first and second operands
- `0B13` **BIT_NOT** `~` [in: _:int] [out: _:int] — Returns a signed number calculated by logical negation of each bit of the input value
- `0B14` **MOD** `%` [in: _:int, _:int] [out: _:int] — Returns the modulo; remainder of a division, after the first number is divided by the second number
- `0B15` **BIT_SHR** `>>` [in: value:int, n:int] [out: _:int] — Returns a number calculated by shifting right all the bits of the value by n bits
- `0B16` **BIT_SHL** `<<` [in: value:int, n:int] [out: _:int] — Returns a number calculated by shifting left all the bits of the value by n bits
- `0B17` **BIT_AND_COMPOUND** `&` [in: _:int, _:int] — Reads a value from the variable, performs bitwise AND operation on it and the operand (BIT_AND) and stores the result back to the variable
- `0B18` **BIT_OR_COMPOUND** `|` [in: _:int, _:int] — Reads a value from the variable, performs bitwise OR operation on it and the operand (BIT_OR) and stores the result back to the variable
- `0B19` **BIT_XOR_COMPOUND** `^` [in: _:int, _:int] — Reads a value from the variable, performs bitwise XOR operation on it and the operand (BIT_XOR) and stores the result back to the variable
- `0B1A` **BIT_NOT_COMPOUND** `~` [in: _:int] — Reads a value from the variable, performs bitwise NOT operation on it (BIT_NOT) and stores the result back to the variable
- `0B1B` **MOD_COMPOUND** `%` [in: _:int, number:int] — Reads a value from the variable, divides it by the number and stores the remainder (MOD) back to the variable
- `0B1C` **BIT_SHR_COMPOUND** `>>` [in: _:int, n:int] — Reads a value from the variable, shifts right by n bits (BIT_SHR) and stores the result back to the variable
- `0B1D` **BIT_SHL_COMPOUND** `<<` [in: _:int, n:int] — Reads a value from the variable, shifts left by n bits (BIT_SHL) and stores the result back to the variable

## Extensión: `math` (13 comandos)

### Math
- `2700` **IS_BIT_SET** (.IsBitSet) [in: number:int, bitIndex:int] _condition, static_ — Checks if n-th bit of the number is set
- `2701` **SET_BIT** (.SetBit) [in: number:int, bitIndex:int] _static_ — Sets n-th bit of the number
- `2702` **CLEAR_BIT** (.ClearBit) [in: number:int, bitIndex:int] _static_ — Clears n-th bit of the number
- `2703` **TOGGLE_BIT** (.ToggleBit) [in: number:int, bitIndex:int, state:bool] _static_ — Sets state of n-th bit in the number
- `2704` **IS_TRUTHY** (.IsTruthy) [in: value:any] _condition, static_ — Checks if value contains number different than 0 or not empty string
- `2705` **PICK_RANDOM_INT** (.RandomPick) [in: values:arguments] [out: result:int] _static_ — Selects one random integer from provided values
- `2706` **PICK_RANDOM_FLOAT** (.RandomPick) [in: values:arguments] [out: result:float] _static_ — Selects one random float from provided values
- `2707` **PICK_RANDOM_TEXT** (.RandomPick) [in: values:arguments] [out: result:string] _static_ — Selects one random text from provided values
- `2708` **RANDOM_CHANCE** (.RandomChance) [in: percent:float] _condition, static_ — Sets random condition result, with percent chance to be true

### (sin clase)
- `2709` **FLOAT_ADD** `+` [in: _:float, _:float] [out: _:float] — Adds together two float values and writes the result into the variable
- `270A` **FLOAT_SUB** `-` [in: _:float, _:float] [out: _:float] — Subtracts the float value from another float value and writes the result into the variable
- `270B` **FLOAT_MUL** `*` [in: _:float, _:float] [out: _:float] — Multiplies two float values and writes the result into the variable
- `270C` **FLOAT_DIV** `/` [in: _:float, _:float] [out: _:float] — Divides the float value by another float value and writes the result into the variable

---
## Extensión: `memory` (8 comandos)

### Memory
- `2400` **COPY_MEMORY** (.Copy) [in: src:int, dest:int, size:int] _static_ — Copies a block of memory from src address to dest address. src and dest regions may overlap (memmove behavior)
- `2401` **READ_MEMORY_WITH_OFFSET** (.ReadWithOffset) [in: address:int, offset:int, size:int] [out: result:int] _static_ — Reads a value from the given offset from the memory address (see: 2402)
- `2402` **WRITE_MEMORY_WITH_OFFSET** (.WriteWithOffset) [in: address:int, offset:int, size:int, value:any] _static_ — Writes the value at the given offset from the memory address (see: 2401)
- `2403` **FORGET_MEMORY** (.Forget) [in: address:int] _static_ — Makes the memory chunk allocated with 0AC8 persistent across load/start new game events. The memory is still released when game closes causing no leaks
- `2404` **GET_SCRIPT_STRUCT_JUST_CREATED** (.GetScriptStructJustCreated) [out: address:int] _static_ — Returns the address of a most recently (globally) created script (004F, 00D7, 0A92, 0A94)
- `2405` **IS_SCRIPT_RUNNING** (.IsScriptRunning) [in: address:int] _condition, static_ — Checks if address points at valid and running script
- `2407` **IS_MEMORY_EQUAL** (.IsEqual) [in: addressA:int, addressB:int, size:int] _condition, static_ — Compares two memory blocks

### (sin clase)
- `2408` **TERMINATE_SCRIPT** [in: address:int] — Terminates script pointed by the address

---
## Extensión: `text` (10 comandos)

### Text
- `2600` **IS_TEXT_EMPTY** (.IsEmpty) [in: string:string] _condition, static_ — Checks if string length is equal to zero
- `2601` **IS_TEXT_EQUAL** (.IsEqual) [in: text:string, another:string, ignoreCase:bool] _condition, static_ — Compares two texts
- `2602` **IS_TEXT_IN_TEXT** (.Contains) [in: text:string, subText:string, ignoreCase:bool] _condition, static_ — Checks if text contains specified text
- `2603` **IS_TEXT_PREFIX** (.StartsWith) [in: text:string, prefix:string, ignoreCase:bool] _condition, static_ — Checks if text starts with specified prefix text
- `2604` **IS_TEXT_SUFFIX** (.EndsWith) [in: text:string, suffix:string, ignoreCase:bool] _condition, static_ — Checks if text ends with specified suffix text
- `2605` **DISPLAY_TEXT_FORMATTED** (.DisplayFormatted) [in: offsetLeft:float, offsetTop:float, format:string, args:arguments] _static_ — Formats args according to the format string then draws text at the specified on-screen position. See 033E
- `2606` **LOAD_FXT** (.LoadFxt) [in: filepath:string] _condition, static_ — Loads GXT texts from selected FXT dictionary file
- `2607` **UNLOAD_FXT** (.UnloadFxt) [in: filepath:string] _condition, static_ — Unloads GXT labels defined in selected Fxt file
- `2608` **GET_TEXT_LENGTH** (.GetLength) [in: text:string] [out: length:int] _static_ — Returns count of characters in the text
- `2609` **ADD_TEXT_LABEL_FORMATTED** (.AddLabelFormatted) [in: dynamicKey:string, format:string, args:arguments] _static_ — Adds or updates the text associated with the dynamic GXT key. It does nothing if the same key is defined in a FXT file
